### Round 3: San Marino Grand Prix
*Date: 1986-04-27*

#### Qualifying Results

### Round 10: German Grand Prix
*Date: 1986-07-27*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |
